     <script>
      (function(){
			window.addEventListener( 'DOMContentLoaded', function() {
				var buttons = document.querySelectorAll( '.hero-desktop__button-container' );
				var sections = document.querySelectorAll( '.hero-desktop__section' );

				for ( var i = 0, len = buttons.length; i < len; i++ ) {
					buttons[i].addEventListener( 'mouseenter', function( ev ) {
						var index = parseInt( this.dataset.id, 10 );
						changeSection( sections, index );
					} );

					buttons[i].addEventListener( 'focusin', function( ev ) {
						var index = parseInt( this.dataset.id, 10 );
						changeSection( sections, index );
					} );
				}

				function changeSection( sections, index ) {
					for ( var i = 0, len = sections.length; i < len; i++ ) {
						sections[i].className = 'hero-desktop__section';

						if ( i === index ) {
							sections[i].className = sections[i].className + ' hero-desktop__section--visible';
						}
					}
				}
			} )
		}());
     </script>

       <div class="content">
